6 min
The Rukn of Qiyas: 'Illah as a Sign (Alam) for the Ruling
Defining the rukn of qiyas and the dispute over the 'illah's scope

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the definition of the 'illah as the rukn of qiyas and explain the Hanafi position that it is a sign (alam) only for the branch (far') and not for the original (asl).

Core Idea
The 'illah is a sign (alam) of the ruling, not its cause; only Allah is the true efficient cause.

In this passage, we explore the foundational pillar (rukn) of qiyas: the 'illah (cause/ratio legis). The author clarifies that the 'illah is not an independent cause but a sign (alam) that points to the ruling contained in the text. A key dispute among usul scholars is whether this sign functions in the original (asl) as well as the branch (far'). The Hanafi mashayikh affirm that the 'illah is a sign only for the branch, because the text itself is the definitive proof for the original. Understanding this distinction is crucial for properly applying qiyas without undermining the authority of primary texts.

Guided Path
1
Identify the rukn of qiyas
Locate the sentence that defines the rukn (pillar) of qiyas. Note that it is described as 'what is made a sign (alam) of the ruling of the text' and is called the comprehensive meaning ('illah).
The term 'rukn' here refers to the essential component without which qiyas does not exist.
2
Understand why it is called 'illah and 'alam
Read the explanation: it is called 'illah because qiyas depends on it; it is called 'alam because the 'illahs of Shariah are indicators (amarat) and definers of the ruling. Emphasize that the true cause is Allah alone.
The author uses 'alam to avoid implying that the 'illah creates the ruling.
3
Analyze the dispute: scope of the 'illah
Find the ikhtilaf: does the 'illah serve as a sign only in the branch (far') or also in the original (asl)? The Hanafi mashayikh hold the first view; the second view is attributed to unnamed scholars.
The 'apparent' (zahir) is the first view according to the Hanafi mashayikh.
4
Examine the Hanafi proof
The Hanafi proof: the text (nass) is a definitive (qat'i) proof for the original; attributing the ruling to the text is more appropriate. The 'illah is only used in the branch out of necessity (where no text exists).
This preserves the authority of the revealed text.
5
Note the pillars of qiyas
From the passage, list the four pillars of qiyas: asl (original), far' (branch), 'illah (cause), and hukm (ruling). Understand that the 'illah is the central pillar.
The author then begins to describe two types of 'illah: necessary (lazim) and accidental ('arid).

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
وَرُكْنُهُ مَا جُعِلَ عَلَمًا عَلَى حُكْمِ النَّصِّ وَهُوَ الْمَعْنَى الْجَامِعُ الْمُسَمَّى عِلَّةً سُمِّيَ رُكْنًا لِأَنَّ مَدَارَ الْقَيَاسِ عَلَيْهِ لَا يَقُومُ الْقَيَاسُ إِلَّا بِهِ وَسُمِّيَ عَلَمًا لِأَنَّ عِلَلَ الشَّرْعِ أَمَارَاتٌ وَمُعَرِّفَاتٌ لِلْحُكْمِ وَعَلَامَاتُهُ عَلَيْهِ وَالْمُوجِبُ الْحَقِيقِيُّ هُوَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى وَإِنَّمَا اخْتَلَفُوا أَنَّ ذَلِكَ الْمَعْنَى عَلَمٌ عَلَى الْحُكْمِ فِي الْفَرْعِ فَقَطْ أَمْ فِي الْأَصْلِ أَيْضًا وَالظَّاهِرُ هُوَ الْأَوَّلُ عَلَى مَا ذَهَبَ إِلَيْهِ مَشَائِخُ الْفِرَاقِ لِأَنَّ النَّصَّ دَلِيلٌ قَطْعِيٌّ وَإِضَافَةُ الْحُكْمِ إِلَيْهِ فِي الْأَصْلِ أَوْلَى مِنْ إِضَافَتِهِ إِلَى الْعِلَّةِ وَإِنَّمَا أُضِيفَ فِي الْفَرْعِ إِلَيْهَا لِلضَّرُورَةِ حَيْثُ لَمْ يُوجَدْ فِيهِ النَّصُّ وَقِيلَ أُضِيفَ حُكْمُ الْأَصْلِ وَالْفَرْعِ جَمِيعًا إِلَى الْعِلَّةِ لِأَنَّهُ مَا لَمْ يَكُنْ تَأْثِيرٌ فِي الْأَصْلِ كَيْفَ تُؤْثِرُ فِي الْفَرْعِ مِمَّا اشْتَمَلَ عَلَيْهِ النَّصُّ أَيْ حَالَ كَوْنِهِ ذَلِكَ الْعِلْمُ مِمَّا اشْتَمَلَ عَلَيْهِ النَّصُّ إِمَّا كَاشْتِمَالِ نَصِّ الرِّبَا عَلَى الْكَيْلِ وَالْجِنْسِ أَوْ بِغَيْرِ صِيغَتِهِ كَاشْتِمَالِ النَّهْيِ عَنْ بَيْعِ الْآبِقِ عَلَى الْعَجْزِ عَنِ التَّسْلِيمِ وَجَعَلَ الْفَرْعَ نَظِيرًا لَهُ أَي لِلْأَصْلِ فِي حُكْمِهِ لِوُجُودِ ذَلِكَ الْمَعْنَى فِيهِ أَيْ وُجُودِ ذَلِكَ الْمَعْنَى فِي الْفَرْعِ وَيُفْهَمُ مِنْ هَذَا أَنَّ أَرْكَانَ الْقَيَاسِ أَرْبَعَةٌ الْأَصْلُ وَالْفَرْعُ وَالْعِلَّةُ وَالْحُكْمُ وَإِنْ كَانَ أَصْلُ الرُّكْنِ هُوَ الْعِلَّةُ ثُمَّ شَرَعَ فِي بَيَانِ أَنَّ ذَلِكَ الْمَعْنَى يَكُونُ عَلَى عِدَّةِ أَنْحَاءٍ فَقَالَ وَهُوَ ثُمَّ جَائِرٌ أَنْ يَكُونَ وَصْفًا لَازِمًا وَعَارِضًا فَالْوَصْفُ اللَّازِمُ أَنْ لَا يَنْفَكَّ عَنِ الْأَصْلِ
And its rukn (pillar) is what is made a sign (alam) for the ruling of the text, and it is the comprehensive meaning called 'illah (cause). It is called rukn because the basis of qiyas is upon it; qiyas does not stand except by it. And it is called 'alam because the 'illahs of the Shariah are indicators and definers of the ruling and its signs. And the true efficient cause is Allah the Exalted. They only differed whether that meaning is a sign for the ruling in the branch (far') only or also in the original (asl). And the apparent (zahir) is the first, according to what the mashayikh of the firqah (Hanafi scholars) held, because the text (nass) is a definitive proof, and attributing the ruling to it in the original is more appropriate than attributing it to the 'illah. It is only attributed to it in the branch out of necessity where the text is not found in it. And it was said that the ruling of both original and branch is attributed to the 'illah, because if there is no effect in the original, how would it effect in the branch? From what the text contains, i.e., in the state of that 'illah being from what the text contains, either like the inclusion of the riba text on measure (kayl) and type (jins), or by other than its wording, like the inclusion of the prohibition of selling a runaway slave on the inability to deliver, and he made the branch a parallel (nazir) to it, i.e., to the original in its ruling, because of the existence of that meaning in it, i.e., the existence of that meaning in the branch. And it is understood from this that the pillars of qiyas are four: the original, the branch, the 'illah, and the ruling, although the main pillar is the 'illah. Then he began to explain that that meaning is of several types, and said: 'And it, then, may be a necessary (lazim) or accidental ('arid) description. So the necessary description is that which does not separate from the original.'
Source pages p. 140

Commentary
This passage defines the rukn (pillar) of qiyas as the 'illah (cause), which is a sign (alam) indicating the ruling in the text. The 'illah is the comprehensive meaning that connects the original and branch. It is called rukn because qiyas depends entirely on it, and 'alam because the 'illah serves as an indicator of the Shariah ruling; the true cause of rulings is Allah alone. A dispute is then mentioned: does the 'illah serve as a sign only in the branch (far') or also in the original (asl)? The preferred view (according to the Hanafi mashayikh) is that it is only a sign in the branch, because the text itself is a definitive proof for the original ruling; attributing the ruling directly to the text is more appropriate. The 'illah is only used in the branch where no text exists. The other view holds that the 'illah indicates the ruling in both original and branch, arguing that if the 'illah had no effect in the original, it could not affect the branch. The author then summarizes that the pillars of qiyas are four: asl, far', 'illah, and hukm, though the core pillar is the 'illah. Finally, he introduces types of 'illah: it can be a necessary (lazim) description that never departs from the original, or an accidental ('arid) description. The passage then begins to discuss the necessary type.

Key Terms
ركن (rukn): Pillar or essential component; here it refers to the 'illah as the core of qiyas.
علم (alam): A sign or indicator; the 'illah is a sign of the ruling, not its cause.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to the Hanafi position presented in the text, why is the 'illah considered a sign only for the branch (far') and not for the original (asl)?
A) Because the original is proven by a definitive text, so attributing the ruling to the text is more appropriate.
B) Because the 'illah is not suitable for the original.
C) Because the original has no ruling.
D) Because the branch is more important.

Key Takeaway
The rukn of qiyas is the 'illah, which is a sign (alam) of the ruling, not its cause; in the Hanafi view, this sign applies only to the branch, preserving the text's primary authority.

Definition and Types of 'Illah in Qiyas
Defining 'illah and classifying it into lazim and 'arid

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the Hanafi definition of 'illah as a sign ('alamah), explain why the Iraqi mashayikh attribute the ruling in the asl to the text, and differentiate between wasf lazim and wasf 'arid with examples from zakat and wudu.

Core Idea
The 'illah is a sign indicating the ruling, not a true cause; in Hanafi usul, the text is the primary source for the asl, and the 'illah operates only in the far'.

In this passage from Nur al-Anwar, the author lays out the fundamental definition of 'illah (the cause/sign) in qiyas. He then presents a crucial debate among Hanafi usulis about whether the ruling in the original (asl) is attributed to the text or to the 'illah. Finally, he classifies the 'illah into two types: essential (lazim) and accidental ('arid), using concrete examples from zakat on gold and silver and wudu due to istihadah. This lesson will help you grasp these foundational concepts.

Guided Path
1
Understand the definition of 'illah
Read the opening line: 'And its pillar is what is made a sign over the ruling of the original.' Identify that the 'illah is defined as a sign ('alamah) that points to the ruling of the asl. This is the Hanafi view, distinguishing it from the Mutakallimun's definition as a cause.
The key term is 'علمًا' (a sign).
2
Analyze the dispute over attribution of the ruling
The text presents two views: (1) The Iraqi mashayikh hold that in the asl, the ruling is attributed to the text (nas), and only in the far' to the 'illah due to necessity. (2) Another view attributes the ruling in both asl and far' to the 'illah. Note the reasoning for the first view: the text is a definitive proof (qat'i), so it is more appropriate to attribute the ruling to it.
The text says: 'لأن النص دليل قطعي'.
3
See how the 'illah is derived from the text
The text explains that the 'illah is taken from what the text encompasses, either by explicit mention (like kayl and jins in the riba verse) or by implication (like the prohibition of selling a runaway slave indicating inability to deliver). This shows how the 'illah is extracted from the nas.
Both ways are valid for Hanafi usul.
4
Identify the four pillars of qiyas
From the statement that the branch is made a counterpart to the original in its ruling due to the presence of the meaning, the text concludes that the pillars of qiyas are four: asl, far', 'illah, and hukm. The 'illah is considered the essential pillar.
The four rukn are derived from the analysis.
5
Classify 'illah into lazim and 'arid
The text then divides the 'illah (the meaning) into two types: lazim (essential/inseparable) and 'arid (accidental). For lazim, study the example of thamaniyyah (monetary value) as the cause for zakat on gold and silver; it is inseparable. For 'arid, study 'bursting' (infijar) as the cause for wudu in istihadah; it may or may not be present.
Be mindful of the cross-madhhab note: al-Shafi'i uses thamaniyyah for riba, while Hanafis use it for zakat.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
وَرُكْنُهُ مَا جُعِلَ عَلَمًا عَلَى حُكْمِ الْأَصْلِ. وَالظَّاهِرُ هُوَ الْأَوَّلُ عَلَى مَا ذَهَبَ إِلَيْهِ مَشَائِخُ الْعِرَاقِ لِأَنَّ النَّصَّ دَلِيلٌ قَطْعِيٌّ وَإِضَافَةُ الْحُكْمِ إِلَيْهِ فِي الْأَصْلِ أَوْلَى مِنْ إِضَافَتِهِ إِلَى الْعِلَّةِ وَإِنَّمَا أُضِيفَ فِي الْفَرْعِ إِلَيْهَا لِلضَّرُورَةِ حَيْثُ لَمْ يُوجَدْ فِيهِ النَّصُّ وَقِيلَ أُضِيفَ حُكْمُ الْأَصْلِ وَالْفَرْعِ جَمِيعًا إِلَى الْعِلَّةِ لِأَنَّهُ مَا لَمْ يَكُنْ تَأْثِيرٌ فِي الْأَصْلِ كَيْفَ يُؤَثِّرُ فِي الْفَرْعِ. مِمَّا اشْتَمَلَ عَلَيْهِ النَّصُّ إِمَّا كَاشْتِمَالِ نَصِّ الرِّبَا عَلَى الْكَيْلِ وَالْجِنْسِ أَوْ بِغَيْرِ صِيغَتِهِ كَاشْتِمَالِ النَّهْيِ عَنْ بَيْعِ الْآبِقِ عَلَى الْعَجْزِ عَنِ التَّسْلِيمِ. وَجُعِلَ الْفَرْعُ نَظِيرًا لَهُ أَيْ لِلْأَصْلِ فِي حُكْمِهِ لِوُجُودِهِ فِيهِ أَيْ وُجُودِ ذَلِكَ الْمَعْنَى فِي الْفَرْعِ. وَيُفْهَمُ مِنْ هَذَا أَنَّ أَرْكَانَ الْقِيَاسِ أَرْبَعَةٌ الْأَصْلُ وَالْفَرْعُ وَالْعِلَّةُ وَالْحُكْمُ وَإِنْ كَانَ أَصْلُ الرُّكْنِ هُوَ الْعِلَّةُ. ثُمَّ شَرَعَ فِي بَيَانِ أَنَّ ذَلِكَ الْمَعْنَى يَكُونُ عَلَى أَنْحَاءٍ فَقَالَ وَهُوَ ثُمَّ جَائِرٌ أَنْ يَكُونَ وَصْفًا لَازِمًا وَعَارِضًا. فَالْوَصْفُ اللَّازِمُ أَنْ لَا يَنْفَكَّ عَنِ الْأَصْلِ كَالثَّمَنِيَّةِ عِلَّةٌ لِوُجُوبِ الزَّكَاةِ فِي الذَّهَبِ وَالْفِضَّةِ لَا يَنْفَكُّ عَنْهُمَا لِأَنَّهُمَا خُلِقَا فِي الْأَصْلِ عَلَى مَعْنَى الثَّمَنِيَّةِ وَهِيَ مُشْتَرَكَةٌ بَيْنَ مَضْرُوبِ الذَّهَبِ وَالْفِضَّةِ وَتِبْرِهِمَا وَحُلِيِّهِمَا فَيَكُونُ فِي حُلِيِّ النِّسَاءِ الزَّكَاةُ لِعِلَّةِ الثَّمَنِيَّةِ وَالشَّافِعِيُّ يُعَلِّلُ حُرْمَةَ الرِّبَا بِهَا وَهِيَ غَيْرُ مُتَعَدِّيَةٍ إِلَى شَيْءٍ. وَالْوَصْفُ الْعَارِضُ كَالْإِنْفِجَارِ فِي قَوْلِهِ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ فَإِنَّهَا دَمُ عِرْقٍ انْفَجَرَ عِلَّةٌ لِوُجُوبِ الْوُضُوءِ فِي الْمُسْتَحَاضَةِ وَهِيَ عَارِضَةٌ لِلدَّمِ إِذْ لَا يَلْزَمُ أَنْ يَكُونَ كُلُّ دَمِ الْعِرْقِ مُنْفَجِرًا فَأَيْنَمَا وُجِدَ انْفِجَارُ الدَّمِ سَوَاءٌ كَانَ لِلْمُسْتَحَاضَةِ أَوْ لِغَيْرِهَا مِنْ غَيْرِ السَّبِيلَيْنِ يَجِبُ بِهِ الْوُضُوءُ.
And its pillar is what is made a sign over the ruling of the original. The apparent (position) is the first, according to what the Iraqi masters went to, because the text is a definitive proof, and attributing the ruling to it in the original is more appropriate than attributing it to the cause; rather, it is attributed to it in the branch out of necessity where no text is found in it. And it was said: the ruling of the original and the branch are both attributed to the cause, because if there is no effect in the original, how can it effect in the branch? From what the text encompasses, either like the inclusion of the riba text on measure and type, or by other than its wording, like the inclusion of the prohibition of selling the runaway slave on the inability to deliver. And the branch was made a counterpart to it, i.e., to the original in its ruling, due to its presence in it, i.e., the presence of that meaning in the branch. And from this it is understood that the pillars of qiyas are four: the original, the branch, the cause, and the ruling, even if the essential pillar is the cause. Then he began explaining that that meaning occurs in several ways, so he said: And it is possible for it to be a description, either essential or accidental. As for the essential description, it is that which is inseparable from the original, like 'being a medium of exchange' (thamaniyyah) as a cause for the obligation of zakat on gold and silver; it is inseparable from them because they were originally created for the meaning of thamaniyyah, and it is common among coined gold and silver, their ore, and their ornaments; thus zakat is due on women's ornaments due to the cause of thamaniyyah. And al-Shafi'i uses it as a cause for the prohibition of riba, and it is not transitive to anything else. As for the accidental description, like 'bursting' in his statement (peace be upon him): 'Indeed, it is a blood vessel that burst' as a cause for the obligation of wudu in the mustahadah; and it is accidental to blood, for it is not necessary that every blood vessel be bursting; so wherever the bursting of blood is found, whether from the mustahadah or from other than her from other than the two passages, wudu becomes obligatory.
Source pages p. 141

Commentary
This passage is from a commentary on Nur al-Anwar, defining the 'illah (cause/sign) in qiyas. The author first states that the 'illah is a sign ('alamah) placed on the ruling of the original (asl). There is a dispute: the preferred view (of the Iraqi mashayikh) is that in the asl, the ruling is attributed to the text (nas) directly, not to the 'illah, because the text is definitive. Only in the far' (branch) is the ruling attributed to the 'illah due to necessity, since there is no direct text. Another view attributes the ruling in both asl and far' to the 'illah, otherwise how could it effect in the far' if it doesn't effect in the asl? The text then explains that the 'illah is derived from what the text encompasses, either explicitly (like the mention of kayl and jins in riba) or implicitly (like the prohibition of selling a runaway slave indicating inability to deliver). The branch is made analogous to the asl due to the presence of the same meaning. From this, the four pillars of qiyas are derived: asl, far', 'illah, and hukm, with the 'illah being the essential pillar. Then the author classifies the 'illah into two types: lazim (essential/inseparable) and 'arid (accidental). An example of lazim: thamaniyyah (monetary value) is an inseparable attribute of gold and silver, making zakat obligatory on them and their ornaments. Note that al-Shafi'i uses thamaniyyah for riba prohibition, but in Hanafi, it is specifically for zakat. An example of 'arid: 'bursting' (infijar) in the hadith about istihadah is accidental, not always present; wherever bursting occurs, wudu becomes obligatory, regardless of the person.

Key Terms
العلة (al-'illah): مَا جُعِلَ عَلَمًا عَلَى حُكْمِ الْأَصْلِ (what is made a sign over the ruling of the original)
الوصف اللازم (al-wasf al-lazim): ما لا ينفك عن الأصل (what is inseparable from the original)
الوصف العارض (al-wasf al-'arid): ما يعرض وقد لا يعرض (what occurs and may not occur)

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to the Hanafi usul text, why is it more appropriate to attribute the ruling in the original (asl) to the text (nas) rather than to the 'illah?
A) Because the text is shorter and easier to memorize
B) Because the text is a definitive proof (qat'i)
C) Because the 'illah is always unknown in the asl
D) Because the asl does not have a ruling

Key Takeaway
In Hanafi usul, the 'illah is defined as a sign ('alamah) on the ruling of the original; it is classified into lazim (essential) and 'arid (accidental), and in the asl, the ruling is attributed to the text, not the 'illah.

Al-Qiyas — Analogical Reasoning
intermediate
8 min
Necessary and Accidental Descriptions as 'Illah
Classifying the 'illah as lazim or 'arid

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to distinguish between a necessary (lazim) and accidental ('arid) description as an 'illah in qiyas, and apply each to a Hanafi fiqh scenario.

Core Idea
A description that never leaves its original is necessary; one that may be absent is accidental – both can be valid causes in Hanafi qiyas.

The Hanafi school classifies the 'illah by how consistently it attaches to its original. A necessary description, like thamaniyya in gold and silver, is inseparable. An accidental description, like the gushing of blood in istihadah, may or may not be present. Understanding this distinction is crucial for determining the scope of qiyas and resolving inter-madhhab disputes.

Guided Path
1
Identify the two categories
Understand that descriptions can be necessary (lazim) – always present in the original – or accidental ('arid) – may be absent.
2
Analyze thamaniyya as necessary
Thamaniyya (being a price) is inseparable from gold and silver; hence zakat is obligatory on all forms including jewelry. This is the Hanafi position.
Shafi'i limits thamaniyya to riba only.
3
Analyze infijar as accidental
Gushing of blood is not essential to blood; yet when present, it triggers the obligation of wudu as per the hadith 'innaha damu 'irqin infajara'.
The cause is the gushing, not the blood itself.
4
Note the inter-madhhab dispute
The Hanafi extension of thamaniyya to zakat is contested by Shafi'i, who views it as a confined cause (qasira) only for riba.
Practical result: Hanafi obligates zakat on jewelry; Shafi'i does not.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
وہ ہے جو اصل سے بھی جدا نہ ہو جیسے شمنیہ ( شمن ہونا) قیمت ہونا) ہونے اور چاندی میں زکوۃ کے واجب ہونے کی علت ہے۔ جو ان دونوں میں بھی جدا نہیں ہوتی کیونکہ ان کی تخلیق ہی شمعیت کے لئے ہوتی ہے اور ثمنیت جس طرح سونا چاندی کی ڈلی میں موجود ہے اسی طرح ان سے بنے ہوئے زیورات، بر تن ، وغیرہ میں بھی پائی جاتی ہے لہذا عورتوں کے سونے اور چاندی کے زیوارت میں علت ثمنیت کی وجہ سے زکوۃ واجب ہو گی۔ اور امام شافل ثمنیت کو وجوب زکوۃ کی علت نہیں بلکہ حرمت ریوا کی علت قرار دیتے ہیں۔ لہذا ان کے نزدیک یہ علت قاصرہ ہے اس لئے نصوص کے علاوہ فرع کی طرف ان کا حکم متعدی نہیں ہوتا۔ وصف عارض کی مثال انفجار ہے ( جاری ہونا ۔ بہتا ) آنحضور صلی اللہ علیہ وسلم کے فرمان فانها دم عرق انفجر ( یہ رگ کا بہتا ہوا خون ہے ) مستحاضہ کے لئے وضوء واجب ہونے کی علت بنائی گئی ہے اور جاری ہونا بہنا یہ خون کا وصف عارض ہے کیونکہ یہ ضروری نہیں ہے کہ ہر دم عرق بہنے والا ہی ہو ۔ لہذا جہاں کہیں انفجار دم پایا جائے گا مستحاضہ عدت کا ہو یا اس کے علاوہ کا یا سمیلین (بول و براز کے راستے) کے علاوہ ہرن کے دوسرے حصوں سے چارمی ہو تو وضو واجب ہو جائے گا۔ وَاسْمًا عَطَفٌ عَلَى قَوْلِهِ وَصَفًا وَمُقَابِلُ لَهُ أَن يَجُوزُ أَنْ يَكُونَ ذَالِكَ الْمَعْنَى إِسْمًا كَالدَّمِ فِى عَيْنِ هَذَا مِثَالِ وَهُوَ قَوْلُهُ عَلَيْهِ السَّلامُ فَإِنَّهَا دَمُ عِرْقٍ انْفَجَرَ فَإِنَّهُ إِنْ اُعْتُبِرَ فِيْهِ لَفْظُ الدَّم كَانَ مِثَالاً لِلاِسْم وَإنْ أَعْتُبِرَ فِيْهِ مَعْنَى الْإِنْفِجَارِ كَانَ مِثَالاً لِلْوَصفِ الْعَارِضِ كَمَا مَرَّ وَجَلِيًّا وَخَفِيًا الظَّاهِرُ أَنَّهُ تَفْسِيمُ لِلْوَصفِ كَلازِم وَالْعَارِضَ فَالْوَصْف الْجَلِي هُوَ مَا يَفْهَمُهُ كُلُّ اَحَدٍ كَالطَّوَافِ لِسَوْرٍ الْهِرَّةِ فِي قَوْلِهِ عَلَيْهِ السَّلاَمُ إِنَّهَا مِنَ الطَّوَّافِينَ وَالطَّوَّافَاتِ عَلَيْكُمْ وَالْوَصْف الْخَفِيُّ هُوَ مَا يَفْهَمُ بَعْضٍ دُونَ بَعْضٍ كَمَا فِي عِلَّةِ الرَّبَوَا عِنْدَنَا الْقَدْرُ وَالْجِنْسُ وَعِنْدَ الشَّافِعِي الطِّعْمُ فِي الْمَطْعُومَاتِ وَالثَّمَنِيَةُ فِي الْأَثْمَانِ وَعِنْدَ مَالِكَ الأَقْتِيَاتُ وَالاِدْخَارُ وَحُكْمًا هَذَا مَعْطَوْفٌ وَمُقَاتِلُ لَهُ أَى يَجُورُ أَنْ يَكُونَ ذَالِكَ الْمَعْنى حُكْمًا شَرْعِيًا جَامِعًا بَيْنَ الأصْلِ وَالفَرْعِ كَمَا رُوِيَ أَنْ أَمْرَاءَ : جَاءَ تَ إِلَى رَسُولِ اللهِ صلى الله عَلَيْهِ وَسَلَّمَ فَقَالَتْ إِنْ أبِي قَدْ أَدْرَكَهُ الْحَج وَهُوَ شَيْخ كَبِيرُ لاَ يَسْتَمْسِكُ عَلَى الرَّاحِلَةِ أَفَتُجِيزُنِي أَنْ أَحَج عَنْهُ فَقَالَ أَرَأَيْتَ لَوْ كَانَ عَلَى أَبِيْك دَيْنٌ فَقَيْصَيْتِهِ آمَا كَانَ يُقْبَلُ مِنْهُ قَالَتْ نَعَمْ قَالَ فَدَيْنُ اللهِ أَحَق بِالْقَبُول فَقَالَ النَّبِيُّ صَلَّى اللهُ عَلَيْهِ وَسَلَمَ الْحَجْ عَلَى دَيْنِ الْعِبَادِ وَالْمَعْنَى الْجَامِعُ بَيْنَهُما هُوَ الدِّينُ وَهُوَ عِبَارَةٌ عَنْ حَقٌّ ثَابِت فِى الدَّمَةِ وَاجِبُ الآدَاءِ وَالْوُجُوبُ حُكْمٌ شَرْعِيٌّ وَفَرْدًا وَعَدَدَا الظَّاهِرُ أَنَّهُ أَيْضًا تَقْسِيمَ لِلْوَصْفِ فَالْوَصَفُ الْفُرْدُ كَالْعِلْةِ بِالْقَدْرِ وَحْدَهُ أَوْ الْجِنْسِ وَحْدَهُ لِحُرْمَةِ النَّسَاءِ وَالْوَصْف الْعَدَدُ كَالْقَدْرِ مَعَ الجِنْسِ عِلةُ لِحُرْمَةِ التفاضل واسما اور جاتا ہے کہ وہ اسم ہو یہ وصفا پر عطف ہے اور اس کا مقابل بھی ہے یعنی جائز ہے ترجمه تشریح کہ وہ وصف ملت ہونے کے بجائے اسم ہو۔ جیسے کہ لفظ دم عید اسی مثال میں یعنی نبی علیہ الام الصلوۃ والسلام کے قول فانها دم عرق کبیر میں کیونکہ اگر اس تعلیل میں لفظ دم کا لحاظ کر لیا جائے تو علت کے اسم ہونے کی مثال بن جائے گی اور اگر جاری ہونے اور بہنے کے وصف کا لحاظ کر لیا جائے تو یہی وصف عارض کی مثال بن جائے گی جیسے کہ گذر چکا ہے۔ جلياً وخفیا خواہ وہ جلی ہو ( واضح) ہو یا خفی ہو بظاہر یہ وصف کی تقسیم ہے جیسے وصف کی ایک تقسیم لازم و عارض ہے ایسے ہی دوسری تقسیم ملی و خفی کی ہے پس وصف جلی وہ ہے جس کو ہر کوئی جان لے اور اس کو سمجھ نے جیسے علت طواف سور ھرہ میں (بلی کا بچا ہوا) آنحضور صلی اللہ علیہ وسلم کے قول انها من الطوافين صلی والطوافات . عليكم ( يہ بلی تمہارے گھروں میں بہت زیادہ آمد ورفت رکھنے والی ہے ) اس لئے اگر اس سے جھوٹے کو نجس قرار دیا جائے تو حرج لازم آئے گا۔ اور وصف کے مخفی، پوشیدہ ہونے کا مطلب یہ ہے کہ جس کو کچھ لوگ ( خواص سمجھیں اور کچھ لوگ (عوام) نہ سمجھ سکیں جیسے ربوا کی علت ہمارے نزدیک قدر اور جنس ہے اور امام شافعی کے نزدیک طعم مطعومات میں ہے تو سونے چاندکی پر ثمنیت علمت ہے اور امام مالک کے نزدیک از دخار ہے (کچھ دن کے لئے ذخیرہ کر لینا) علت ہے وحکما اور جائز ہے کہ وہ حکم ہو اس کا عطف مصنف کے قول وصفا پر ہے اور وصف ہی کے مقابل بھی ہے یعنی یہ کہ جائز ہے کہ معنی (علت) حکم شرعی ہو جو اصل اور فرح میں یکساں پایا جائے جیسے روایت میں ہے کہ ایک عورت جناب رسول اللہ صلی اللہ علیہ وسلم کی خدمت میں حاضر ہوئی اور کہا میرے باپ نے زمانہ حج پالیا ہے اور وہ بوڑھے ضعیف ہیں کجاوہ (سواری) پر بیٹھے نہیں سکتے ہیں پس کیا آپ مجھے اجازت دیتے ہیں کہ میں ان کی طرف سے حج کرلوں تو حضور صلی اللہ علیہ وسلم نے جواب دیا اچھا بتاؤ اگر تمہارے باپ کے اوپر قرض ہو تا تو تم اس کی طرف سے ادائے گی کرتی یا نہ کرتیں۔ کیا یہ ادائیگی قرضن تمہاری طرف سے قبول نہ کیا جاتا ہو لیں ہاں یا رسول اللہ تو آنحضور صلی اللہ علیہ وسلم نے بیج کو بندوں کے قرض پر قیاس فرمایا ہے اور ان دونوں کے درمیان علت مشترکہ دینا ہے دین زمہ میں حق کے ثابت ہونے کا نام ہے جس کی ادئیگی واجب ہوتی ہے اور وجوب حکم شرع ہے۔ جس کو آپ نے دوسرے حکم شرعی یعنی قبول عند الادار کے لئے علت قرار دیا ہے فرداً وعدد أخواہ منفرد ہو یا متعدد ہو بظاہر یہ بھی وصف کے اقسام ہیں۔ وصف فرد کی مثال جیسے وہ تنہا علت جنس عورتوں کے حرام ہونے کے
It is that which is not separate from the original, like thamaniyya (being a price, value) is the cause for the obligation of zakat on gold and silver. It does not separate from both of them because their creation is for being a price, and thamaniyya is present in gold and silver bullion similarly in ornaments, vessels, etc. made from them, hence zakat is obligatory on women's gold and silver ornaments due to the cause of thamaniyya. Imam al-Shafi'i does not consider thamaniyya as the cause for obligation of zakat but as the cause for prohibition of riba. Hence in his view this cause is qasira (confined) so its ruling does not extend to a branch beyond the texts. Example of an accidental description is infijar (gushing, flowing) in the Prophet's (peace be upon him) saying 'indeed it is a blood of a gushing vein' made as a cause for obligation of wudu for mustahada. And gushing/flowing is an accidental description of blood because it is not necessary that every blood of a vein gushes. So wherever blood gushing is found, whether from mustahada of 'idda or otherwise, or from other parts of the animal except the two passages (urine and feces), if it flows? then wudu becomes obligatory. 'And as a name' is coordinated with his saying 'and as a description' and is its opposite, meaning it is permissible that that meaning be a name, like blood in the same example, and it is his saying (peace be upon him) 'indeed it is a blood of a gushing vein'. If in it the word 'blood' is considered, it becomes an example of a name; if the meaning of gushing is considered, it becomes an example of accidental description as mentioned. 'And manifest and hidden' apparently it is a division of description like necessary and accidental. So manifest description is that which everyone understands, like the frequenting of the cat in his saying (peace be upon him) 'indeed it is of those who go about among you'. And hidden description is that which some understand and others not, like the cause of riba with us is quantity and genus, and with al-Shafi'i is food-ness in foodstuffs and thamaniyya in valuables, and with Malik is staples and storage. 'And as a ruling' this is coordinated and opposite to it, i.e., it is permissible that that meaning be a legal ruling uniting the original and branch, as narrated that a woman came to the Messenger of Allah (peace be upon him) and said: 'My father has caught the time of hajj and he is an old man who cannot sit firmly on the mount, so do you permit me to perform hajj on his behalf?' He said: 'What do you think, if your father had a debt and you paid it, would it be accepted from him?' She said: 'Yes.' He said: 'Then the debt of Allah is more deserving of acceptance.' So the Prophet (peace be upon him) made qiyas of hajj on the debt of servants, and the common meaning between them is 'dayn' (debt), which is a term for a right established in the liability, obligatory to discharge, and obligation is a legal ruling. 'And singular and plural' apparently this too is a division of description. So singular description is like the cause by quantity alone or genus alone for prohibition of women, and plural description is like quantity with genus as a cause for prohibition of excess. 'And as a name' it comes that it is a name; this is coordinated with his saying 'and as a description' and is its opposite, meaning it is permissible that that description instead of being a description be a name, like the word 'blood' in this example, i.e., in the Prophet's saying 'indeed it is a blood of a gushing vein'. Because if in this ta'lil the word 'blood' is considered, it becomes an example of the cause being a name, and if the description of gushing and flowing is considered, it becomes an example of an accidental description as passed. 'And manifest and hidden' whether it is manifest (clear) or hidden, apparently this is a division of description, just as one division of description is necessary and accidental, similarly another division is manifest and hidden. So manifest description is that which everyone knows and understands, like the cause of frequenting in the cat's leftover (the cat is one of those who go about among you). The Prophet (peace be upon him) said: 'Indeed it is of those who go about among you' meaning this cat goes around your houses a lot, so if its leftover is considered impure, hardship would follow. And hidden description means that some people (elite) understand it and some (commoners) do not, like the cause of riba with us is quantity and genus, and with al-Shafi'i is taste in foodstuffs, and thamaniyya on gold and silver is the cause, and with Malik is staples and storage. 'And as a ruling' it is permissible that it be a ruling; this is coordinated and opposite to his saying 'and as a description', meaning it is permissible that the meaning (cause) be a legal ruling that is found equally in original and branch, as in the narration that a woman came to the Messenger of Allah (peace be upon him) and said: 'My father has caught the time of hajj and he is an old man who cannot sit on the mount, so do you permit me to perform hajj on his behalf?' The Prophet (peace be upon him) replied: 'Tell me, if your father had a debt and you paid it, would it be accepted from you?' She said: 'Yes.' He said: 'Then the debt of Allah is more deserving of acceptance.' The Prophet (peace be upon him) made qiyas of hajj on the debt of servants, and the common meaning between them is 'dayn', which is a term for a right established in the liability, obligatory to discharge, and obligation is a legal ruling. 'And singular and plural' it says whether singular or plural; apparently this too is a division of description. So singular description is like the cause by quantity alone or genus alone for prohibition of marriage, and plural description is like quantity with genus as a cause for prohibition of excess.
Source pages p. 143

Commentary
This passage from Ashraf al-Anwar, a commentary on Nur al-Anwar, classifies the 'illah (cause/effective cause) in qiyas according to multiple categories. It begins by illustrating a necessary (lazim) description: thamaniyya (the quality of being a price or standard of value) is the cause for zakat on gold and silver. Since thamaniyya is inherent in both bullion and jewelry, zakat is obligatory on both. This is contrasted with Imam al-Shafi'i's view, who restricts thamaniyya to riba, making it a confined cause (qasira) that does not extend beyond the texts. The accidental ('arid) description is then exemplified by the gushing of blood in istihadah; the flow (infijar) is not essential to blood but accidental, yet when present, it triggers the ruling of wudu. Next, the passage discusses whether the 'illah can be a name (ism) or a description (wasf). Using the same hadith, if one considers the word 'blood' it is a name; if one considers the meaning of gushing it is a description. Then the distinction between manifest (jali) and hidden (khafi) descriptions is explained: manifest is understood by all (e.g., a cat's frequenting is obvious), while hidden is understood only by some (e.g., quantity and genus as cause for riba, disputed among madhahib). Finally, the ruling (hukm) can serve as the 'illah itself, as in the hadith where the common meaning of debt (dayn) – a right in the liability – is used to analogize hajj. The description can be singular (fard) as in quantity alone, or multiple (adad) as in quantity with genus. The commentary enriches each distinction with Hanafi examples and inter-madhhab disputes.

Key Terms
الثمنية (ath-thamaniyya): The quality of being a price or standard of value; the effective cause for zakat on gold and silver in Hanafi usul.
الوصف العارض (al-wasf al-ʿāriḍ): An accidental attribute that may or may not be present; used as 'illah when occurring, e.g., gushing (infijar) in blood.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
What key difference distinguishes a necessary (lazim) description from an accidental ('arid) description as 'illah?
A) Lazim is always present; 'arid is sometimes absent.
B) Lazim is understood only by scholars; 'arid is obvious.
C) Lazim can only be used in ibadat; 'arid in muamalat.
D) Lazim is a name; 'arid is a description.

Key Takeaway
In Hanafi usul, both necessary and accidental descriptions can serve as 'illah, but their scope differs: necessary extends to all instances, accidental only where the attribute occurs.

Al-Qiyas — Analogical Reasoning
intermediate
6 min
The 'Illah as a Name or a Description
Exploring the 'illah as a lexical entity

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to differentiate between an 'illah that is a name (ism) and one that is a description (wasf), using the Hanafi example of blood and gushing.

Core Idea
The same linguistic expression can be treated as a name or a description, allowing flexibility in ta'lil.

In Hanafi usul, the 'illah can be identified either as a concrete name (like 'blood') or as a description (like 'gushing'). The choice depends on which meaning the mujtahid considers decisive. This distinction affects how the 'illah is applied across cases.

Guided Path
1
Understand the two possibilities
The 'illah may be taken as a name (ism) – a noun – or as a description (wasf) – an attribute derived from a verb or meaning.
2
Analyze the hadith of istihadah
In 'innaha damu 'irqin infajara', the word 'dam' (blood) is a name; the meaning of 'infijar' (gushing) is a description.
Both are valid approaches.
3
Apply the distinction
If the name is taken, the 'illah is the substance itself; if the description, it is the attribute. This affects the scope of qiyas.
Using the name restricts analogy to that specific entity; using the description allows extending to similar attributes.

جائے گا۔ وَاسْمًا عَطَفٌ عَلَى قَوْلِهِ وَصَفًا وَمُقَابِلُ لَهُ أَن يَجُوزُ أَنْ يَكُونَ ذَالِكَ الْمَعْنَى إِسْمًا كَالدَّمِ فِى عَيْنِ هَذَا مِثَالِ وَهُوَ قَوْلُهُ عَلَيْهِ السَّلامُ فَإِنَّهَا وَخَفِيًا الظَّاهِرُ أَنَّهُ تَفْسِيمُ لِلْوَصفِ كَلازِم وَالْعَارِضَ فَالْوَصْف الْجَلِي هُوَ مَا يَفْهَمُهُ كُلُّ اَحَدٍ كَالطَّوَافِ لِسَوْرٍ الْهِرَّةِ فِي قَوْلِهِ عَلَيْهِ السَّلاَمُ إِنَّهَا مِنَ الطَّوَّافِينَ وَالطَّوَّافَاتِ عَلَيْكُمْ وَالْوَصْف الْخَفِيُّ هُوَ مَا يَفْهَمُ بَعْضٍ دُونَ بَعْضٍ كَمَا فِي عِلَّةِ الرَّبَوَا عِنْدَنَا الْقَدْرُ وَالْجِنْسُ وَعِنْدَ الشَّافِعِي الطِّعْمُ النَّسَاءِ وَالْوَصْف الْعَدَدُ كَالْقَدْرِ مَعَ الجِنْسِ عِلةُ لِحُرْمَةِ التفاضل واسما اور جاتا ہے کہ وہ اسم ہو یہ وصفا پر عطف ہے اور اس کا مقابل بھی ہے یعنی جائز ہے ترجمه تشریح کہ وہ وصف ملت ہونے کے بجائے اسم ہو۔ جیسے کہ لفظ دم عید اسی مثال میں یعنی نبی علیہ الام الصلوۃ والسلام کے قول فانها دم عرق کبیر میں کیونکہ اگر اس تعلیل میں لفظ دم کا لحاظ کر لیا جائے تو علت کے اسم ہونے کی مثال بن جائے گی اور اگر جاری ہونے اور بہنے کے وصف کا لحاظ کر لیا جائے تو یہی وصف عارض کی مثال بن جائے گی جیسے کہ گذر چکا ہے۔ جلياً وخفیا خواہ وہ جلی ہو ( واضح) ہو یا خفی ہو بظاہر یہ وصف کی تقسیم ہے جیسے وصف کی ایک تقسیم لازم و عارض ہے ایسے ہی دوسری تقسیم ملی و خفی کی ہے پس وصف جلی وہ ہے جس کو ہر کوئی جان لے اور اس کو سمجھ نے جیسے علت طواف سور ھرہ میں (بلی کا بچا ہوا) آنحضور صلی اللہ علیہ وسلم کے قول انها من الطوافين صلی والطوافات . عليكم ( يہ بلی تمہارے گھروں میں بہت زیادہ آمد ورفت رکھنے والی ہے ) اس لئے اگر اس سے جھوٹے کو نجس قرار دیا جائے تو حرج لازم آئے گا۔ اور وصف کے مخفی، پوشیدہ ہونے کا مطلب یہ ہے کہ جس کو کچھ لوگ ( خواص سمجھیں اور کچھ لوگ (عوام) نہ سمجھ سکیں جیسے ربوا کی علت ہمارے نزدیک قدر اور جنس ہے اور امام شافعی کے نزدیک طعم مطعومات میں ہے تو سونے چاندکی پر ثمنیت علمت ہے اور امام مالک کے نزدیک از دخار ہے (کچھ دن کے لئے ذخیرہ کر لینا) علت ہے وحکما اور جائز ہے کہ وہ حکم ہو اس کا عطف مصنف کے قول وصفا پر ہے اور وصف ہی کے مقابل بھی ہے یعنی یہ کہ جائز ہے کہ معنی (علت) حکم شرعی ہو جو اصل اور فرح میں یکساں پایا جائے جیسے روایت میں ہے کہ ایک عورت جناب رسول اللہ صلی اللہ علیہ وسلم کی خدمت میں حاضر ہوئی اور کہا میرے باپ نے زمانہ حج پالیا ہے اور وہ بوڑھے ضعیف ہیں کجاوہ (سواری) پر بیٹھے نہیں سکتے ہیں پس کیا آپ مجھے اجازت دیتے ہیں کہ میں ان کی طرف سے حج کرلوں تو حضور صلی اللہ علیہ وسلم نے جواب دیا اچھا بتاؤ اگر تمہارے باپ کے اوپر قرض ہو تا تو تم اس کی طرف سے ادائے گی کرتی یا نہ کرتیں۔ کیا یہ ادائیگی قرضن تمہاری طرف سے قبول نہ کیا جاتا ہو لیں ہاں یا رسول اللہ تو آنحضور صلی اللہ علیہ وسلم نے بیج کو بندوں کے قرض پر قیاس فرمایا ہے اور ان دونوں کے درمیان علت مشترکہ دینا ہے دین زمہ میں حق کے ثابت ہونے کا نام ہے جس کی ادئیگی واجب ہوتی ہے اور وجوب حکم شرع ہے۔ جس کو آپ نے دوسرے حکم شرعی یعنی قبول عند الادار کے لئے علت قرار دیا ہے فرداً وعدد أخواہ منفرد ہو یا متعدد ہو بظاہر یہ بھی وصف کے اقسام ہیں۔ وصف فرد کی مثال جیسے وہ تنہا علت جنس عورتوں کے حرام ہونے کے
It is that which is not separate from the original, like thamaniyya (being a price, value) is the cause for the obligation of zakat on gold and silver. It does not separate from both of them because their creation is for being a price, and thamaniyya is present in gold and silver bullion similarly in ornaments, vessels, etc. made from them, hence zakat is obligatory on women's gold and silver ornaments due to the cause of thamaniyya. Imam al-Shafi'i does not consider thamaniyya as the cause for obligation of zakat but as the cause for prohibition of riba. Hence in his view this cause is qasira (confined) so its ruling does not extend to a branch beyond the texts. Example of an accidental description is infijar (gushing, flowing) in the Prophet's (peace be upon him) saying 'indeed it is a blood of a gushing vein' made as a cause for obligation of wudu for mustahada. And gushing/flowing is an accidental description of blood because it is not necessary that every blood of a vein gushes. So wherever blood gushing is found, whether from mustahada of 'idda or otherwise, or from other parts of the animal except the two passages (urine and feces), if it flows? then wudu becomes obligatory. 'And as a name' is coordinated with his saying 'and as a description' and is its opposite, meaning it is permissible that that meaning be a name, like blood in the same example, and it is his saying (peace be upon him) 'indeed it is a blood of a gushing vein'. If in it the word 'blood' is considered, it becomes an example of a name; if the meaning of gushing is considered, it becomes an example of accidental description as mentioned. 'And manifest and hidden' apparently it is a division of description like necessary and accidental. So manifest description is that which everyone understands, like the frequenting of the cat in his saying (peace be upon him) 'indeed it is of those who go about among you'. And hidden description is that which some understand and others not, like the cause of riba with us is quantity and genus, and with al-Shafi'i is food-ness in foodstuffs and thamaniyya in valuables, and with Malik is staples and storage. 'And as a ruling' this is coordinated and opposite to it, i.e., it is permissible that that meaning be a legal ruling uniting the original and branch, as narrated that a woman came to the Messenger of Allah (peace be upon him) and said: 'My father has caught the time of hajj and he is an old man who cannot sit firmly on the mount, so do you permit me to perform hajj on his behalf?' He said: 'What do you think, if your father had a debt and you paid it, would it be accepted from him?' She said: 'Yes.' He said: 'Then the debt of Allah is more deserving of acceptance.' So the Prophet (peace be upon him) made qiyas of hajj on the debt of servants, and the common meaning between them is 'dayn' (debt), which is a term for a right established in the liability, obligatory to discharge, and obligation is a legal ruling. 'And singular and plural' apparently this too is a division of description. So singular description is like the cause by quantity alone or genus alone for prohibition of women, and plural description is like quantity with genus as a cause for prohibition of excess. 'And as a name' it comes that it is a name; this is coordinated with his saying 'and as a description' and is its opposite, meaning it is permissible that that description instead of being a description be a name, like the word 'blood' in this example, i.e., in the Prophet's saying 'indeed it is a blood of a gushing vein'. Because if in this ta'lil the word 'blood' is considered, it becomes an example of the cause being a name, and if the description of gushing and flowing is considered, it becomes an example of an accidental description as passed. 'And manifest and hidden' whether it is manifest (clear) or hidden, apparently this is a division of description, just as one division of description is necessary and accidental, similarly another division is manifest and hidden. So manifest description is that which everyone knows and understands, like the cause of frequenting in the cat's leftover (the cat is one of those who go about among you). The Prophet (peace be upon him) said: 'Indeed it is of those who go about among you' meaning this cat goes around your houses a lot, so if its leftover is considered impure, hardship would follow. And hidden description means that some people (elite) understand it and some (commoners) do not, like the cause of riba with us is quantity and genus, and with al-Shafi'i is taste in foodstuffs, and thamaniyya on gold and silver is the cause, and with Malik is staples and storage. 'And as a ruling' it is permissible that it be a ruling; this is coordinated and opposite to his saying 'and as a description', meaning it is permissible that the meaning (cause) be a legal ruling that is found equally in original and branch, as in the narration that a woman came to the Messenger of Allah (peace be upon him) and said: 'My father has caught the time of hajj and he is an old man who cannot sit on the mount, so do you permit me to perform hajj on his behalf?' The Prophet (peace be upon him) replied: 'Tell me, if your father had a debt and you paid it, would it be accepted from you?' She said: 'Yes.' He said: 'Then the debt of Allah is more deserving of acceptance.' The Prophet (peace be upon him) made qiyas of hajj on the debt of servants, and the common meaning between them is 'dayn', which is a term for a right established in the liability, obligatory to discharge, and obligation is a legal ruling. 'And singular and plural' it says whether singular or plural; apparently this too is a division of description. So singular description is like the cause by quantity alone or genus alone for prohibition of marriage, and plural description is like quantity with genus as a cause for prohibition of excess.
Source pages p. 143

Commentary
This passage from Ashraf al-Anwar, a commentary on Nur al-Anwar, classifies the 'illah (cause/effective cause) in qiyas according to multiple categories. It begins by illustrating a necessary (lazim) description: thamaniyya (the quality of being a price or standard of value) is the cause for zakat on gold and silver. Since thamaniyya is inherent in both bullion and jewelry, zakat is obligatory on both. This is contrasted with Imam al-Shafi'i's view, who restricts thamaniyya to riba, making it a confined cause (qasira) that does not extend beyond the texts. The accidental ('arid) description is then exemplified by the gushing of blood in istihadah; the flow (infijar) is not essential to blood but accidental, yet when present, it triggers the ruling of wudu. Next, the passage discusses whether the 'illah can be a name (ism) or a description (wasf). Using the same hadith, if one considers the word 'blood' it is a name; if one considers the meaning of gushing it is a description. Then the distinction between manifest (jali) and hidden (khafi) descriptions is explained: manifest is understood by all (e.g., a cat's frequenting is obvious), while hidden is understood only by some (e.g., quantity and genus as cause for riba, disputed among madhahib). Finally, the ruling (hukm) can serve as the 'illah itself, as in the hadith where the common meaning of debt (dayn) – a right in the liability – is used to analogize hajj. The description can be singular (fard) as in quantity alone, or multiple (adad) as in quantity with genus. The commentary enriches each distinction with Hanafi examples and inter-madhhab disputes.

Key Terms
اسم (ism): A noun used as the 'illah, e.g., 'blood' in the hadith.
وصف (wasf): A description or attribute used as the 'illah, e.g., 'gushing'.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
What is the difference between taking the 'illah as a name vs as a description?
A) A name is always the cause; a description is not.
B) A name refers to a concrete thing; a description refers to an attribute.
C) A name is only used in muamalat; a description in ibadat.
D) A name is more specific; a description is more general.

Key Takeaway
The same ta'lil can be based on either the substantive name or the attributive description, offering flexibility in analogical reasoning.

Al-Qiyas — Analogical Reasoning
intermediate
8 min
Manifest and Hidden Descriptions in Ta'lil
Distinguishing jali from khafi in qiyas

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to distinguish a manifest (jali) description from a hidden (khafi) one, and explain the Hanafi position on the 'illah for riba.

Core Idea
A manifest description is clear to all; a hidden one requires ijtihad – as in the debated causes for riba.

Descriptions can be ranked by clarity. Manifest descriptions, like a cat’s frequenting, are obvious to everyone. Hidden descriptions, like quantity and genus for riba, are understood only by specialists. The Hanafi school holds that quantity and genus are the 'illah for riba, whereas Shafi'is and Malikis propose other hidden descriptions. This leads to different rulings on gold and silver transactions.

Guided Path
1
Understand manifest description
A manifest (jali) description is understood by all without special training, e.g., the cat's frequenting in the hadith about its leftover water.
Everyone knows cats go around houses.
2
Understand hidden description
A hidden (khafi) description is understood only by those with ijtihad, e.g., the 'illah for riba. Hanafis say it is quantity and genus; Shafi'is say taste and thamaniyya; Malikis say staples and storage.
These are not obvious to laypeople.
3
Examine the Hanafi 'illah for riba
Hanafis use quantity (qadr) and genus (jins) as the compound cause, preventing unequal exchanges within the same genus.
This applies to all commodities, not just food.
4
Compare with other schools
Shafi'is use taste in foodstuffs and thamaniyya in precious metals; Malikis use staples and storage. Each 'illah yields a different scope of prohibition.
Practical rulings differ accordingly.

Source Text

وہ ہے جو اصل سے بھی جدا نہ ہو جیسے شمنیہ ( شمن ہونا) قیمت ہونا) ہونے اور چاندی میں زکوۃ کے واجب ہونے کی علت ہے۔ جو ان دونوں میں بھی جدا نہیں ہوتی کیونکہ ان کی تخلیق ہی شمعیت کے لئے ہوتی ہے اور ثمنیت جس طرح سونا چاندی کی ڈلی میں موجود ہے اسی طرح ان سے بنے ہوئے زیورات، بر تن ، وغیرہ میں بھی پائی جاتی ہے لہذا عورتوں کے سونے اور چاندی کے زیوارت میں علت ثمنیت کی وجہ سے زکوۃ واجب ہو گی۔ اور امام شافل ثمنیت کو وجوب زکوۃ کی علت نہیں بلکہ حرمت ریوا کی علت قرار دیتے ہیں۔ لہذا ان کے نزدیک یہ علت قاصرہ ہے اس لئے نصوص کے علاوہ فرع کی طرف ان کا حکم متعدی نہیں ہوتا۔ وصف عارض کی مثال انفجار ہے ( جاری ہونا ۔ بہتا ) آنحضور صلی اللہ علیہ وسلم کے فرمان فانها دم عرق انفجر ( یہ رگ کا بہتا ہوا خون ہے ) مستحاضہ کے لئے وضوء واجب ہونے کی علت بنائی گئی ہے اور جاری ہونا بہنا یہ خون کا وصف عارض ہے کیونکہ یہ ضروری نہیں ہے کہ ہر دم عرق بہنے والا ہی ہو ۔ لہذا جہاں کہیں انفجار دم پایا جائے گا مستحاضہ عدت کا ہو یا اس کے علاوہ کا یا سمیلین (بول و براز کے راستے) کے علاوہ ہرن کے دوسرے حصوں سے چارمی ہو تو وضو واجب ہو جائے گا۔ وَاسْمًا عَطَفٌ عَلَى قَوْلِهِ وَصَفًا وَمُقَابِلُ لَهُ أَن يَجُوزُ أَنْ يَكُونَ ذَالِكَ الْمَعْنَى إِسْمًا كَالدَّمِ فِى عَيْنِ هَذَا مِثَالِ وَهُوَ قَوْلُهُ عَلَيْهِ السَّلامُ فَإِنَّهَا دَمُ عِرْقٍ انْفَجَرَ فَإِنَّهُ إِنْ اُعْتُبِرَ فِيْهِ لَفْظُ الدَّم كَانَ مِثَالاً لِلاِسْم وَإنْ أَعْتُبِرَ فِيْهِ مَعْنَى الْإِنْفِجَارِ كَانَ مِثَالاً لِلْوَصفِ الْعَارِضِ كَمَا مَرَّ وَجَلِيًّا وَخَفِيًا الظَّاهِرُ أَنَّهُ تَفْسِيمُ لِلْوَصفِ كَلازِم وَالْعَارِضَ فَالْوَصْف الْجَلِي هُوَ مَا يَفْهَمُهُ كُلُّ اَحَدٍ كَالطَّوَافِ لِسَوْرٍ الْهِرَّةِ فِي قَوْلِهِ عَلَيْهِ السَّلاَمُ إِنَّهَا مِنَ الطَّوَّافِينَ وَالطَّوَّافَاتِ عَلَيْكُمْ وَالْوَصْف الْخَفِيُّ هُوَ مَا يَفْهَمُ بَعْضٍ دُونَ بَعْضٍ كَمَا فِي عِلَّةِ الرَّبَوَا عِنْدَنَا الْقَدْرُ وَالْجِنْسُ وَعِنْدَ الشَّافِعِي الطِّعْمُ فِي الْمَطْعُومَاتِ وَالثَّمَنِيَةُ فِي الْأَثْمَانِ وَعِنْدَ مَالِكَ الأَقْتِيَاتُ وَالاِدْخَارُ وَحُكْمًا هَذَا مَعْطَوْفٌ وَمُقَاتِلُ لَهُ أَى يَجُورُ أَنْ يَكُونَ ذَالِكَ الْمَعْنى حُكْمًا شَرْعِيًا جَامِعًا بَيْنَ الأصْلِ وَالفَرْعِ كَمَا رُوِيَ أَنْ أَمْرَاءَ : جَاءَ تَ إِلَى رَسُولِ اللهِ صلى الله عَلَيْهِ وَسَلَّمَ فَقَالَتْ إِنْ أبِي قَدْ أَدْرَكَهُ الْحَج وَهُوَ شَيْخ كَبِيرُ لاَ يَسْتَمْسِكُ عَلَى الرَّاحِلَةِ أَفَتُجِيزُنِي أَنْ أَحَج عَنْهُ فَقَالَ أَرَأَيْتَ لَوْ كَانَ عَلَى أَبِيْك دَيْنٌ فَقَيْصَيْتِهِ آمَا كَانَ يُقْبَلُ مِنْهُ قَالَتْ نَعَمْ قَالَ فَدَيْنُ اللهِ أَحَق بِالْقَبُول فَقَالَ النَّبِيُّ صَلَّى اللهُ عَلَيْهِ وَسَلَمَ الْحَجْ عَلَى دَيْنِ الْعِبَادِ وَالْمَعْنَى الْجَامِعُ بَيْنَهُما هُوَ الدِّينُ وَهُوَ عِبَارَةٌ عَنْ حَقٌّ ثَابِت فِى الدَّمَةِ وَاجِبُ الآدَاءِ وَالْوُجُوبُ حُكْمٌ شَرْعِيٌّ وَفَرْدًا وَعَدَدَا الظَّاهِرُ أَنَّهُ أَيْضًا تَقْسِيمَ لِلْوَصْفِ فَالْوَصَفُ الْفُرْدُ كَالْعِلْةِ بِالْقَدْرِ وَحْدَهُ أَوْ الْجِنْسِ وَحْدَهُ لِحُرْمَةِ النَّسَاءِ وَالْوَصْف الْعَدَدُ كَالْقَدْرِ مَعَ الجِنْسِ عِلةُ لِحُرْمَةِ التفاضل واسما اور جاتا ہے کہ وہ اسم ہو یہ وصفا پر عطف ہے اور اس کا مقابل بھی ہے یعنی جائز ہے ترجمه تشریح کہ وہ وصف ملت ہونے کے بجائے اسم ہو۔ جیسے کہ لفظ دم عید اسی مثال میں یعنی نبی علیہ الام الصلوۃ والسلام کے قول فانها دم عرق کبیر میں کیونکہ اگر اس تعلیل میں لفظ دم کا لحاظ کر لیا جائے تو علت کے اسم ہونے کی مثال بن جائے گی اور اگر جاری ہونے اور بہنے کے وصف کا لحاظ کر لیا جائے تو یہی وصف عارض کی مثال بن جائے گی جیسے کہ گذر چکا ہے۔ جلياً وخفیا خواہ وہ جلی ہو ( واضح) ہو یا خفی ہو بظاہر یہ وصف کی تقسیم ہے جیسے وصف کی ایک تقسیم لازم و عارض ہے ایسے ہی دوسری تقسیم ملی و خفی کی ہے پس وصف جلی وہ ہے جس کو ہر کوئی جان لے اور اس کو سمجھ نے جیسے علت طواف سور ھرہ میں (بلی کا بچا ہوا) آنحضور صلی اللہ علیہ وسلم کے قول انها من الطوافين صلی والطوافات . عليكم ( يہ بلی تمہارے گھروں میں بہت زیادہ آمد ورفت رکھنے والی ہے ) اس لئے اگر اس سے جھوٹے کو نجس قرار دیا جائے تو حرج لازم آئے گا۔ اور وصف کے مخفی، پوشیدہ ہونے کا مطلب یہ ہے کہ جس کو کچھ لوگ ( خواص سمجھیں اور کچھ لوگ (عوام) نہ سمجھ سکیں جیسے ربوا کی علت ہمارے نزدیک قدر اور جنس ہے اور امام شافعی کے نزدیک طعم مطعومات میں ہے تو سونے چاندکی پر ثمنیت علمت ہے اور امام مالک کے نزدیک از دخار ہے (کچھ دن کے لئے ذخیرہ کر لینا) علت ہے وحکما اور جائز ہے کہ وہ حکم ہو اس کا عطف مصنف کے قول وصفا پر ہے اور وصف ہی کے مقابل بھی ہے یعنی یہ کہ جائز ہے کہ معنی (علت) حکم شرعی ہو جو اصل اور فرح میں یکساں پایا جائے جیسے روایت میں ہے کہ ایک عورت جناب رسول اللہ صلی اللہ علیہ وسلم کی خدمت میں حاضر ہوئی اور کہا میرے باپ نے زمانہ حج پالیا ہے اور وہ بوڑھے ضعیف ہیں کجاوہ (سواری) پر بیٹھے نہیں سکتے ہیں پس کیا آپ مجھے اجازت دیتے ہیں کہ میں ان کی طرف سے حج کرلوں تو حضور صلی اللہ علیہ وسلم نے جواب دیا اچھا بتاؤ اگر تمہارے باپ کے اوپر قرض ہو تا تو تم اس کی طرف سے ادائے گی کرتی یا نہ کرتیں۔ کیا یہ ادائیگی قرضن تمہاری طرف سے قبول نہ کیا جاتا ہو لیں ہاں یا رسول اللہ تو آنحضور صلی اللہ علیہ وسلم نے بیج کو بندوں کے قرض پر قیاس فرمایا ہے اور ان دونوں کے درمیان علت مشترکہ دینا ہے دین زمہ میں حق کے ثابت ہونے کا نام ہے جس کی ادئیگی واجب ہوتی ہے اور وجوب حکم شرع ہے۔ جس کو آپ نے دوسرے حکم شرعی یعنی قبول عند الادار کے لئے علت قرار دیا ہے فرداً وعدد أخواہ منفرد ہو یا متعدد ہو بظاہر یہ بھی وصف کے اقسام ہیں۔ وصف فرد کی مثال جیسے وہ تنہا علت جنس عورتوں کے حرام ہونے کے
It is that which is not separate from the original, like thamaniyya (being a price, value) is the cause for the obligation of zakat on gold and silver. It does not separate from both of them because their creation is for being a price, and thamaniyya is present in gold and silver bullion similarly in ornaments, vessels, etc. made from them, hence zakat is obligatory on women's gold and silver ornaments due to the cause of thamaniyya. Imam al-Shafi'i does not consider thamaniyya as the cause for obligation of zakat but as the cause for prohibition of riba. Hence in his view this cause is qasira (confined) so its ruling does not extend to a branch beyond the texts. Example of an accidental description is infijar (gushing, flowing) in the Prophet's (peace be upon him) saying 'indeed it is a blood of a gushing vein' made as a cause for obligation of wudu for mustahada. And gushing/flowing is an accidental description of blood because it is not necessary that every blood of a vein gushes. So wherever blood gushing is found, whether from mustahada of 'idda or otherwise, or from other parts of the animal except the two passages (urine and feces), if it flows? then wudu becomes obligatory. 'And as a name' is coordinated with his saying 'and as a description' and is its opposite, meaning it is permissible that that meaning be a name, like blood in the same example, and it is his saying (peace be upon him) 'indeed it is a blood of a gushing vein'. If in it the word 'blood' is considered, it becomes an example of a name; if the meaning of gushing is considered, it becomes an example of accidental description as mentioned. 'And manifest and hidden' apparently it is a division of description like necessary and accidental. So manifest description is that which everyone understands, like the frequenting of the cat in his saying (peace be upon him) 'indeed it is of those who go about among you'. And hidden description is that which some understand and others not, like the cause of riba with us is quantity and genus, and with al-Shafi'i is food-ness in foodstuffs and thamaniyya in valuables, and with Malik is staples and storage. 'And as a ruling' this is coordinated and opposite to it, i.e., it is permissible that that meaning be a legal ruling uniting the original and branch, as narrated that a woman came to the Messenger of Allah (peace be upon him) and said: 'My father has caught the time of hajj and he is an old man who cannot sit firmly on the mount, so do you permit me to perform hajj on his behalf?' He said: 'What do you think, if your father had a debt and you paid it, would it be accepted from him?' She said: 'Yes.' He said: 'Then the debt of Allah is more deserving of acceptance.' So the Prophet (peace be upon him) made qiyas of hajj on the debt of servants, and the common meaning between them is 'dayn' (debt), which is a term for a right established in the liability, obligatory to discharge, and obligation is a legal ruling. 'And singular and plural' apparently this too is a division of description. So singular description is like the cause by quantity alone or genus alone for prohibition of women, and plural description is like quantity with genus as a cause for prohibition of excess. 'And as a name' it comes that it is a name; this is coordinated with his saying 'and as a description' and is its opposite, meaning it is permissible that that description instead of being a description be a name, like the word 'blood' in this example, i.e., in the Prophet's saying 'indeed it is a blood of a gushing vein'. Because if in this ta'lil the word 'blood' is considered, it becomes an example of the cause being a name, and if the description of gushing and flowing is considered, it becomes an example of an accidental description as passed. 'And manifest and hidden' whether it is manifest (clear) or hidden, apparently this is a division of description, just as one division of description is necessary and accidental, similarly another division is manifest and hidden. So manifest description is that which everyone knows and understands, like the cause of frequenting in the cat's leftover (the cat is one of those who go about among you). The Prophet (peace be upon him) said: 'Indeed it is of those who go about among you' meaning this cat goes around your houses a lot, so if its leftover is considered impure, hardship would follow. And hidden description means that some people (elite) understand it and some (commoners) do not, like the cause of riba with us is quantity and genus, and with al-Shafi'i is taste in foodstuffs, and thamaniyya on gold and silver is the cause, and with Malik is staples and storage. 'And as a ruling' it is permissible that it be a ruling; this is coordinated and opposite to his saying 'and as a description', meaning it is permissible that the meaning (cause) be a legal ruling that is found equally in original and branch, as in the narration that a woman came to the Messenger of Allah (peace be upon him) and said: 'My father has caught the time of hajj and he is an old man who cannot sit on the mount, so do you permit me to perform hajj on his behalf?' The Prophet (peace be upon him) replied: 'Tell me, if your father had a debt and you paid it, would it be accepted from you?' She said: 'Yes.' He said: 'Then the debt of Allah is more deserving of acceptance.' The Prophet (peace be upon him) made qiyas of hajj on the debt of servants, and the common meaning between them is 'dayn', which is a term for a right established in the liability, obligatory to discharge, and obligation is a legal ruling. 'And singular and plural' it says whether singular or plural; apparently this too is a division of description. So singular description is like the cause by quantity alone or genus alone for prohibition of marriage, and plural description is like quantity with genus as a cause for prohibition of excess.
Source pages p. 143

Commentary
This passage from Ashraf al-Anwar, a commentary on Nur al-Anwar, classifies the 'illah (cause/effective cause) in qiyas according to multiple categories. It begins by illustrating a necessary (lazim) description: thamaniyya (the quality of being a price or standard of value) is the cause for zakat on gold and silver. Since thamaniyya is inherent in both bullion and jewelry, zakat is obligatory on both. This is contrasted with Imam al-Shafi'i's view, who restricts thamaniyya to riba, making it a confined cause (qasira) that does not extend beyond the texts. The accidental ('arid) description is then exemplified by the gushing of blood in istihadah; the flow (infijar) is not essential to blood but accidental, yet when present, it triggers the ruling of wudu. Next, the passage discusses whether the 'illah can be a name (ism) or a description (wasf). Using the same hadith, if one considers the word 'blood' it is a name; if one considers the meaning of gushing it is a description. Then the distinction between manifest (jali) and hidden (khafi) descriptions is explained: manifest is understood by all (e.g., a cat's frequenting is obvious), while hidden is understood only by some (e.g., quantity and genus as cause for riba, disputed among madhahib). Finally, the ruling (hukm) can serve as the 'illah itself, as in the hadith where the common meaning of debt (dayn) – a right in the liability – is used to analogize hajj. The description can be singular (fard) as in quantity alone, or multiple (adad) as in quantity with genus. The commentary enriches each distinction with Hanafi examples and inter-madhhab disputes.

Key Terms
الوصف الجلي (al-wasf al-jalī): A manifest description that is understood by everyone without specialization, e.g., the frequenting of a cat.
الوصف الخفي (al-wasf al-khafī): A hidden description that requires ijtihad to discern, e.g., quantity and genus as causes for riba.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
In the Hanafi school, what are the two components of the 'illah for riba in gold and silver?
A) Taste and thamaniyya
B) Quantity and genus
C) Staples and storage
D) Tawaf and infijar

Key Takeaway
The hiddenness of an 'illah does not affect its validity; it only determines who can perceive it. Hanafis use quantity and genus as hidden descriptions for riba.

Al-Qiyas — Analogical Reasoning
intermediate
6 min
When the 'Illah is a Legal Ruling
Exploring the 'illah as a normative concept

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to explain how a legal ruling itself can serve as the 'illah in qiyas, citing the hadith of hajj for a parent.

Core Idea
A legal ruling, such as the obligation of a debt, can be the common element linking two cases in qiyas.

The Hanafi school recognizes that the 'illah does not have to be a physical attribute; it can be a legal ruling (hukm). In the famous hadith of the woman asking about hajj on behalf of her father, the Prophet used the ruling of debt (dayn) – a financial obligation – as the common meaning to justify deputizing in hajj. This demonstrates that a ruling can act as the 'illah.

Guided Path
1
Understand the concept
An 'illah can be a legal ruling (hukm shar'i) that unites the original and branch cases.
The ruling itself becomes the cause for another ruling.
2
Analyze the hadith
A woman asked to perform hajj for her elderly father. The Prophet analogized to debt: if debt can be paid by proxy, so can hajj. The common meaning is 'dayn' (obligation).
Dayn is a right in the liability that must be discharged.
3
Identify the 'illah
The 'illah is the ruling of obligation (wujub) inherent in dayn. This ruling is used to justify permissibility of deputizing in hajj.
Obligation is a legal ruling.

وہ ہے جو اصل سے بھی جدا نہ ہو جیسے شمنیہ ( شمن ہونا) قیمت ہونا) ہونے اور چاندی میں زکوۃ کے واجب ہونے کی علت ہے۔ جو ان دونوں میں بھی جدا نہیں ہوتی کیونکہ ان کی تخلیق ہی شمعیت کے لئے ہوتی ہے اور ثمنیت جس طرح سونا چاندی کی ڈلی میں موجود ہے اسی طرح ان سے بنے ہوئے زیورات، بر تن ، وغیرہ میں بھی پائی جاتی ہے لہذا عورتوں کے سونے اور چاندی کے زیوارت میں علت ثمنیت کی وجہ سے زکوۃ واجب ہو گی۔ اور امام شافل ثمنیت کو وجوب زکوۃ کی علت نہیں بلکہ حرمت ریوا کی علت قرار دیتے ہیں۔ لہذا ان کے نزدیک یہ علت قاصرہ ہے اس لئے نصوص کے علاوہ فرع کی طرف ان کا حکم متعدی نہیں ہوتا۔ وصف عارض کی مثال انفجار ہے ( جاری ہونا ۔ بہتا ) آنحضور صلی اللہ علیہ وسلم کے فرمان فانها دم عرق انفجر ( یہ رگ کا بہتا ہوا خون ہے ) مستحاضہ کے لئے وضوء واجب ہونے کی علت بنائی گئی ہے اور جاری ہونا بہنا یہ خون کا وصف عارض ہے کیونکہ یہ ضروری نہیں ہے کہ ہر دم عرق بہنے والا ہی ہو ۔ لہذا جہاں کہیں انفجار دم پایا جائے گا مستحاضہ عدت کا ہو یا اس کے علاوہ کا یا سمیلین (بول و براز کے راستے) کے علاوہ ہرن کے دوسرے حصوں سے چارمی ہو تو وضو واجب ہو جائے گا۔ وَاسْمًا عَطَفٌ عَلَى قَوْلِهِ وَصَفًا وَمُقَابِلُ لَهُ أَن يَجُوزُ أَنْ يَكُونَ ذَالِكَ الْمَعْنَى إِسْمًا كَالدَّمِ فِى عَيْنِ هَذَا مِثَالِ وَهُوَ قَوْلُهُ عَلَيْهِ السَّلامُ فَإِنَّهَا دَمُ عِرْقٍ انْفَجَرَ فَإِنَّهُ إِنْ اُعْتُبِرَ فِيْهِ لَفْظُ الدَّم كَانَ مِثَالاً لِلاِسْم وَإنْ أَعْتُبِرَ فِيْهِ مَعْنَى الْإِنْفِجَارِ كَانَ مِثَالاً لِلْوَصفِ الْعَارِضِ كَمَا مَرَّ وَجَلِيًّا وَخَفِيًا الظَّاهِرُ أَنَّهُ تَفْسِيمُ لِلْوَصفِ كَلازِم وَالْعَارِضَ فَالْوَصْف الْجَلِي هُوَ مَا يَفْهَمُهُ كُلُّ اَحَدٍ كَالطَّوَافِ لِسَوْرٍ الْهِرَّةِ فِي قَوْلِهِ عَلَيْهِ السَّلاَمُ إِنَّهَا مِنَ الطَّوَّافِينَ وَالطَّوَّافَاتِ عَلَيْكُمْ وَالْوَصْف الْخَفِيُّ هُوَ مَا يَفْهَمُ بَعْضٍ دُونَ بَعْضٍ كَمَا فِي عِلَّةِ الرَّبَوَا عِنْدَنَا الْقَدْرُ وَالْجِنْسُ وَعِنْدَ الشَّافِعِي الطِّعْمُ فِي الْمَطْعُومَاتِ وَالثَّمَنِيَةُ فِي الْأَثْمَانِ وَعِنْدَ مَالِكَ الأَقْتِيَاتُ وَالاِدْخَارُ وَحُكْمًا هَذَا مَعْطَوْفٌ وَمُقَاتِلُ لَهُ أَى يَجُورُ أَنْ يَكُونَ ذَالِكَ الْمَعْنى حُكْمًا شَرْعِيًا جَامِعًا بَيْنَ الأصْلِ وَالفَرْعِ كَمَا رُوِيَ أَنْ أَمْرَاءَ : جَاءَ تَ إِلَى رَسُولِ اللهِ صلى الله عَلَيْهِ وَسَلَّمَ فَقَالَتْ إِنْ أبِي قَدْ أَدْرَكَهُ الْحَج وَهُوَ شَيْخ كَبِيرُ لاَ يَسْتَمْسِكُ عَلَى الرَّاحِلَةِ أَفَتُجِيزُنِي أَنْ أَحَج عَنْهُ فَقَالَ أَرَأَيْتَ لَوْ كَانَ عَلَى أَبِيْك دَيْنٌ فَقَيْصَيْتِهِ آمَا كَانَ يُقْبَلُ مِنْهُ قَالَتْ نَعَمْ قَالَ فَدَيْنُ اللهِ أَحَق بِالْقَبُول فَقَالَ النَّبِيُّ صَلَّى اللهُ عَلَيْهِ وَسَلَمَ الْحَجْ عَلَى دَيْنِ الْعِبَادِ وَالْمَعْنَى الْجَامِعُ بَيْنَهُما هُوَ الدِّينُ وَهُوَ عِبَارَةٌ عَنْ حَقٌّ ثَابِت فِى الدَّمَةِ وَاجِبُ الآدَاءِ وَالْوُجُوبُ حُكْمٌ شَرْعِيٌّ وَفَرْدًا وَعَدَدَا الظَّاهِرُ أَنَّهُ أَيْضًا تَقْسِيمَ لِلْوَصْفِ فَالْوَصَفُ الْفُرْدُ كَالْعِلْةِ بِالْقَدْرِ وَحْدَهُ أَوْ الْجِنْسِ وَحْدَهُ لِحُرْمَةِ النَّسَاءِ وَالْوَصْف الْعَدَدُ كَالْقَدْرِ مَعَ الجِنْسِ عِلةُ لِحُرْمَةِ التفاضل واسما اور جاتا ہے کہ وہ اسم ہو یہ وصفا پر عطف ہے اور اس کا مقابل بھی ہے یعنی جائز ہے ترجمه تشریح کہ وہ وصف ملت ہونے کے بجائے اسم ہو۔ جیسے کہ لفظ دم عید اسی مثال میں یعنی نبی علیہ الام الصلوۃ والسلام کے قول فانها دم عرق کبیر میں کیونکہ اگر اس تعلیل میں لفظ دم کا لحاظ کر لیا جائے تو علت کے اسم ہونے کی مثال بن جائے گی اور اگر جاری ہونے اور بہنے کے وصف کا لحاظ کر لیا جائے تو یہی وصف عارض کی مثال بن جائے گی جیسے کہ گذر چکا ہے۔ جلياً وخفیا خواہ وہ جلی ہو ( واضح) ہو یا خفی ہو بظاہر یہ وصف کی تقسیم ہے جیسے وصف کی ایک تقسیم لازم و عارض ہے ایسے ہی دوسری تقسیم ملی و خفی کی ہے پس وصف جلی وہ ہے جس کو ہر کوئی جان لے اور اس کو سمجھ نے جیسے علت طواف سور ھرہ میں (بلی کا بچا ہوا) آنحضور صلی اللہ علیہ وسلم کے قول انها من الطوافين صلی والطوافات . عليكم ( يہ بلی تمہارے گھروں میں بہت زیادہ آمد ورفت رکھنے والی ہے ) اس لئے اگر اس سے جھوٹے کو نجس قرار دیا جائے تو حرج لازم آئے گا۔ اور وصف کے مخفی، پوشیدہ ہونے کا مطلب یہ ہے کہ جس کو کچھ لوگ ( خواص سمجھیں اور کچھ لوگ (عوام) نہ سمجھ سکیں جیسے ربوا کی علت ہمارے نزدیک قدر اور جنس ہے اور امام شافعی کے نزدیک طعم مطعومات میں ہے تو سونے چاندکی پر ثمنیت علمت ہے اور امام مالک کے نزدیک از دخار ہے (کچھ دن کے لئے ذخیرہ کر لینا) علت ہے وحکما اور جائز ہے کہ وہ حکم ہو اس کا عطف مصنف کے قول وصفا پر ہے اور وصف ہی کے مقابل بھی ہے یعنی یہ کہ جائز ہے کہ معنی (علت) حکم شرعی ہو جو اصل اور فرح میں یکساں پایا جائے جیسے روایت میں ہے کہ ایک عورت جناب رسول اللہ صلی اللہ علیہ وسلم کی خدمت میں حاضر ہوئی اور کہا میرے باپ نے زمانہ حج پالیا ہے اور وہ بوڑھے ضعیف ہیں کجاوہ (سواری) پر بیٹھے نہیں سکتے ہیں پس کیا آپ مجھے اجازت دیتے ہیں کہ میں ان کی طرف سے حج کرلوں تو حضور صلی اللہ علیہ وسلم نے جواب دیا اچھا بتاؤ اگر تمہارے باپ کے اوپر قرض ہو تا تو تم اس کی طرف سے ادائے گی کرتی یا نہ کرتیں۔ کیا یہ ادائیگی قرضن تمہاری طرف سے قبول نہ کیا جاتا ہو لیں ہاں یا رسول اللہ تو آنحضور صلی اللہ علیہ وسلم نے بیج کو بندوں کے قرض پر قیاس فرمایا ہے اور ان دونوں کے درمیان علت مشترکہ دینا ہے دین زمہ میں حق کے ثابت ہونے کا نام ہے جس کی ادئیگی واجب ہوتی ہے اور وجوب حکم شرع ہے۔ جس کو آپ نے دوسرے حکم شرعی یعنی قبول عند الادار کے لئے علت قرار دیا ہے فرداً وعدد أخواہ منفرد ہو یا متعدد ہو بظاہر یہ بھی وصف کے اقسام ہیں۔ وصف فرد کی مثال جیسے وہ تنہا علت جنس عورتوں کے حرام ہونے کے
It is that which is not separate from the original, like thamaniyya (being a price, value) is the cause for the obligation of zakat on gold and silver. It does not separate from both of them because their creation is for being a price, and thamaniyya is present in gold and silver bullion similarly in ornaments, vessels, etc. made from them, hence zakat is obligatory on women's gold and silver ornaments due to the cause of thamaniyya. Imam al-Shafi'i does not consider thamaniyya as the cause for obligation of zakat but as the cause for prohibition of riba. Hence in his view this cause is qasira (confined) so its ruling does not extend to a branch beyond the texts. Example of an accidental description is infijar (gushing, flowing) in the Prophet's (peace be upon him) saying 'indeed it is a blood of a gushing vein' made as a cause for obligation of wudu for mustahada. And gushing/flowing is an accidental description of blood because it is not necessary that every blood of a vein gushes. So wherever blood gushing is found, whether from mustahada of 'idda or otherwise, or from other parts of the animal except the two passages (urine and feces), if it flows? then wudu becomes obligatory. 'And as a name' is coordinated with his saying 'and as a description' and is its opposite, meaning it is permissible that that meaning be a name, like blood in the same example, and it is his saying (peace be upon him) 'indeed it is a blood of a gushing vein'. If in it the word 'blood' is considered, it becomes an example of a name; if the meaning of gushing is considered, it becomes an example of accidental description as mentioned. 'And manifest and hidden' apparently it is a division of description like necessary and accidental. So manifest description is that which everyone understands, like the frequenting of the cat in his saying (peace be upon him) 'indeed it is of those who go about among you'. And hidden description is that which some understand and others not, like the cause of riba with us is quantity and genus, and with al-Shafi'i is food-ness in foodstuffs and thamaniyya in valuables, and with Malik is staples and storage. 'And as a ruling' this is coordinated and opposite to it, i.e., it is permissible that that meaning be a legal ruling uniting the original and branch, as narrated that a woman came to the Messenger of Allah (peace be upon him) and said: 'My father has caught the time of hajj and he is an old man who cannot sit firmly on the mount, so do you permit me to perform hajj on his behalf?' He said: 'What do you think, if your father had a debt and you paid it, would it be accepted from him?' She said: 'Yes.' He said: 'Then the debt of Allah is more deserving of acceptance.' So the Prophet (peace be upon him) made qiyas of hajj on the debt of servants, and the common meaning between them is 'dayn' (debt), which is a term for a right established in the liability, obligatory to discharge, and obligation is a legal ruling. 'And singular and plural' apparently this too is a division of description. So singular description is like the cause by quantity alone or genus alone for prohibition of women, and plural description is like quantity with genus as a cause for prohibition of excess. 'And as a name' it comes that it is a name; this is coordinated with his saying 'and as a description' and is its opposite, meaning it is permissible that that description instead of being a description be a name, like the word 'blood' in this example, i.e., in the Prophet's saying 'indeed it is a blood of a gushing vein'. Because if in this ta'lil the word 'blood' is considered, it becomes an example of the cause being a name, and if the description of gushing and flowing is considered, it becomes an example of an accidental description as passed. 'And manifest and hidden' whether it is manifest (clear) or hidden, apparently this is a division of description, just as one division of description is necessary and accidental, similarly another division is manifest and hidden. So manifest description is that which everyone knows and understands, like the cause of frequenting in the cat's leftover (the cat is one of those who go about among you). The Prophet (peace be upon him) said: 'Indeed it is of those who go about among you' meaning this cat goes around your houses a lot, so if its leftover is considered impure, hardship would follow. And hidden description means that some people (elite) understand it and some (commoners) do not, like the cause of riba with us is quantity and genus, and with al-Shafi'i is taste in foodstuffs, and thamaniyya on gold and silver is the cause, and with Malik is staples and storage. 'And as a ruling' it is permissible that it be a ruling; this is coordinated and opposite to his saying 'and as a description', meaning it is permissible that the meaning (cause) be a legal ruling that is found equally in original and branch, as in the narration that a woman came to the Messenger of Allah (peace be upon him) and said: 'My father has caught the time of hajj and he is an old man who cannot sit on the mount, so do you permit me to perform hajj on his behalf?' The Prophet (peace be upon him) replied: 'Tell me, if your father had a debt and you paid it, would it be accepted from you?' She said: 'Yes.' He said: 'Then the debt of Allah is more deserving of acceptance.' The Prophet (peace be upon him) made qiyas of hajj on the debt of servants, and the common meaning between them is 'dayn', which is a term for a right established in the liability, obligatory to discharge, and obligation is a legal ruling. 'And singular and plural' it says whether singular or plural; apparently this too is a division of description. So singular description is like the cause by quantity alone or genus alone for prohibition of marriage, and plural description is like quantity with genus as a cause for prohibition of excess.
Source pages p. 143

Commentary
This passage from Ashraf al-Anwar, a commentary on Nur al-Anwar, classifies the 'illah (cause/effective cause) in qiyas according to multiple categories. It begins by illustrating a necessary (lazim) description: thamaniyya (the quality of being a price or standard of value) is the cause for zakat on gold and silver. Since thamaniyya is inherent in both bullion and jewelry, zakat is obligatory on both. This is contrasted with Imam al-Shafi'i's view, who restricts thamaniyya to riba, making it a confined cause (qasira) that does not extend beyond the texts. The accidental ('arid) description is then exemplified by the gushing of blood in istihadah; the flow (infijar) is not essential to blood but accidental, yet when present, it triggers the ruling of wudu. Next, the passage discusses whether the 'illah can be a name (ism) or a description (wasf). Using the same hadith, if one considers the word 'blood' it is a name; if one considers the meaning of gushing it is a description. Then the distinction between manifest (jali) and hidden (khafi) descriptions is explained: manifest is understood by all (e.g., a cat's frequenting is obvious), while hidden is understood only by some (e.g., quantity and genus as cause for riba, disputed among madhahib). Finally, the ruling (hukm) can serve as the 'illah itself, as in the hadith where the common meaning of debt (dayn) – a right in the liability – is used to analogize hajj. The description can be singular (fard) as in quantity alone, or multiple (adad) as in quantity with genus. The commentary enriches each distinction with Hanafi examples and inter-madhhab disputes.

Key Terms
حكم (hukm): A legal ruling used as the 'illah, e.g., obligation (wujub) in the hadith.
دين (dayn): A financial obligation or debt; term used as the common meaning in the hadith.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
In the hajj hadith, what is the common meaning (al-ma'na al-jami') used for qiyas?
A) Thamaniyya
B) Infijar
C) Dayn (obligation)
D) Tawaf

Key Takeaway
A legal ruling, such as obligation, can serve as the 'illah, broadening the scope of analogical reasoning.

Al-Qiyas — Analogical Reasoning
intermediate
5 min
Singular and Compound Descriptions as 'Illah
Examining the number of attributes in the 'illah

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to differentiate between a single description and a combination of descriptions as the 'illah, using examples from Hanafi usul.

Core Idea
An 'illah may consist of one attribute or a set of attributes; the combination matters for the scope of analogy.

Descriptions used as causes can be singular (fard) – one attribute alone – or plural ('adad) – a combination of attributes. The Hanafi school illustrates this with the 'illah for riba: quantity and genus together form the compound cause. They also mention a singular cause, but the example given (quantity alone for prohibition of women) requires careful interpretation.

Guided Path
1
Understand the division
Descriptions are divided into singular (fard) and plural ('adad) based on how many attributes constitute the 'illah.
2
Examine the compound example
The Hanafi 'illah for riba is compound: quantity combined with genus. This prevents excess within the same genus.
Both must be present.
3
Examine the singular example
The text gives a singular example: quantity alone or genus alone as cause for prohibition of women (likely a textual issue, but the classification remains).
Singular causes are simpler but may be less precise.
4
Note the practical effect
A compound 'illah is more restrictive; a singular 'illah may allow broader analogy.
